# plan.md ÔÇö Feature scope & build log

> [!IMPORTANT]
> **PRODUCT NAME: CADENCE.** The product is **Cadence**, and that is the only name to use. A brief 2026-06-10 rename experiment to a different brand was reverted on 2026-06-16; the retired name must not be reintroduced anywhere (code, docs, DB, env, caches, APIs). Any stray legacy token from that experiment is to be read as equivalent to `cadence`/`Cadence`.
>
> _Do not perform destructive refactoring of database column/table names or folder structures that are bound to Lovable Cloud and pgvector schemas. All modifications should map the name logically at the user and documentation level while keeping underlying plumbing compatible._

> The canonical record of **what Cadence is built to be** (the full feature scope), **the order we build it**, and **what already exists to reuse**. Product framing: [`README.md`](./README.md). Operating rules: [`AGENTS.md`](./AGENTS.md). Architecture: [`architecture/`](./architecture/). UI contract: [`design.md`](./design.md).
>
> **No MVP1/MVP2/MVP3 gating, no far-future phase deferral.** We build the full intended scope on the current stack ([`docs/decisions/tech-stack.md`](./docs/decisions/tech-stack.md)) and ship continuously. This doc is written to be read straight into a coding session (Claude Code / Lovable) and acted on.

---

## How this file is organized

1. **Feature scope** ÔÇö the whole product, stress-tested as if nothing is built. The high-level feature list.
2. **Competitive feature comparison** ÔÇö factory.ai ┬À hyperagent ┬À Linear ÔåÆ what Cadence should build.
3. **Granular feature catalog** ÔÇö every feature from login/logout to agent-transfer/workspace level, with _what_ and _why_. This is the dev-ready map.
4. **Build order** ÔÇö the sequence to build it, production-grade, reusing legacy code where it fits.
5. **Active build log** ÔÇö what we actually ship, updated as we go (starts near-empty).
6. **Legacy build log (retained)** ÔÇö the previous source build, kept as a reuse reference, not the plan.
7. **Product-agent roster** ÔÇö re-examined (explicit vs. implicit).
8. **Testing, lessons, out-of-scope.**

---

## 1. Feature scope (stress-tested from scratch)

> [!IMPORTANT]
> **v4 supersedes this section for scope (2026-06-11).** The canonical feature scope is now [`docs/strategy/v4-feature-map-2026-06-11.md`](./docs/strategy/v4-feature-map-2026-06-11.md) ÔÇö 7 platform laws, 6 stations over the 12-stage engine, the 19-agent mesh with handoff contract + HITL gate matrix, the 7-surface IA, station feature catalogs (SEN/DEC/DEF/BLD/LCH/LRN/ENG/OPS), and milestones M1ÔÇôM5. The adversarial reasoning behind it: [`docs/strategy/v4-stress-test-2026-06-11.md`](./docs/strategy/v4-stress-test-2026-06-11.md). The 12-stage engine description below remains valid as the _internal_ loop reference; where wording differs, **the v4 map wins**. **v5 overlay (2026-06-11):** the _felt product_ ÔÇö wedge UX, nav, vocabulary, June 22 demo scope ÔÇö is governed by [`docs/strategy/v5-chief-of-staff-2026-06-11.md`](./docs/strategy/v5-chief-of-staff-2026-06-11.md) (PM Chief of Staff; 4 felt surfaces + Trust drawer; phases `F-V5-RITUAL` ÔåÆ `F-V5-DEMO`). v4 remains the expansion map.

Cadence runs the full product lifecycle as one governed, autonomous loop. The scope below is the target product ÔÇö not a discovery tool. Each stage is run by autonomous agents; the human approves at the gates.

### Who we serve, what they expect, and the gap (grounding for the feature list)

The feature list below is a deliberate response to who the customer is and what the market already sets as table-stakes ÔÇö not a wish list. Inspiration drawn from products worth learning from is captured in [`docs/references/competitive-reference.md`](docs/references/competitive-reference.md) (deferred; inspiration only).

**Personas (who orchestrates Cadence):**

- **P1 ÔÇö Enterprise Director / VP of Product (The Portfolio Governor)**: owns portfolio-level alignment, agent spend budgets, and compliance. Pain: Swarm drift, lack of visibility into agent actions, security audits, budget overruns, and multi-product roadmap health.
- **P2 ÔÇö Lead / Senior PM (The Daily Cockpit Operator)**: runs day-to-day discovery, spec definition, and feature delivery. Pain: Mechanical process work (spec writing, ticket updates, release logs, alert triage) eating up time needed for strategic judgment.
- **P3 ÔÇö Engineering Lead / Tech Architect (The Code Gatekeeper)**: guards repository health, code quality, and branch stability. Pain: Agent-written code drifting from internal architecture guidelines, introducing regressions, or breaking sandboxed environments.
- **P4 ÔÇö UX/UI Designer (The Visual Validator)**: ensures design tokens and brand style guide alignment. Pain: Generated code failing to match design system tokens or looking off-brand in mockups.
- **P5 ÔÇö GTM Lead / Product Marketer**: handles positioning and product launch. Pain: Generating changelogs, marketing collateral, newsletter posts, and distribution updates by hand for every release.
- **P6 ÔÇö Customer Success & Support Lead**: monitors product support feedback. Pain: High ticket volumes, slow bug triage, and user signals getting lost before reaching the product manager.

**Market expectations (table-stakes ÔÇö must-haves, or we're not credible):** auth + SSO-ready tenancy; real (not mocked) data; connectors to the tools they live in; an assistant/chat surface; observability + cost visibility; approvals/audit for anything autonomous; multi-project support; export/no-lock-in.

**The gap (where the market is underserved ÔÇö our opening):** point tools own single bands (engineering autonomy, or issue tracking, or research synthesis). **No one runs the _whole_ lifecycle ÔÇö discover ÔåÆ build ÔåÆ ship ÔåÆ launch ÔåÆ support ÔåÆ learn ÔÇö as one governed, autonomous, multi-product loop.** That gap is the spine of the feature catalog in section 2.

**What the customer actually wants (the job):** "Take this intent and run it end-to-end ÔÇö autonomously, in parallel, across my products ÔÇö and only stop me for the calls that matter." Every feature below maps to that job.

**The feature list derives from the PM's actual day.** The product manager is the cockpit operator ÔÇö the features below exist to run the PM's day (triage inbox ÔåÆ decide ÔåÆ synthesize ÔåÆ spec ÔåÆ tickets ÔåÆ build/test/ship ÔåÆ launch/update ÔåÆ answer "why is this on the roadmap?" ÔåÆ report ÔåÆ repeat). The day-to-features mapping and the PM/eng-lead lenses are in [`docs/planning/considerations.md`](docs/planning/considerations.md). If a feature does not serve a real PM task, question it.

### Lifecycle stages (the 12-Stage Product Loop)

**S1 ÔÇö Signal Capture**

- Multi-source signal ingest: support tickets, churn, usage telemetry, sales notes, reviews, NPS, interviews.
- Agent clustering ÔåÆ themes ÔåÆ ICE-scored opportunities; continuous (not one-shot) synthesis; dedupe by similarity.
- A continuously-updated discovery feed per product.

**S2 ÔÇö Audio Sync (WhisperFlow)**

- High-context audio recording, transcription, and meeting spec extraction.
- Translates voice memos or team meetings into feature specs and backlog tickets with zero friction.

**S3 ÔÇö ICE Prioritization**

- Prioritization queue management: opportunity scoring based on Impact, Confidence, and Ease.
- Automated re-prioritization as new signals arrive or existing ones scale in severity.

**S4 ÔÇö Spec Definition**

- Opportunity ÔåÆ PRD/spec, retrieval-grounded and cited; inline `/ai` editing; versioned with diff.
- Acceptance criteria, non-goals, risks, success metrics auto-drafted; human edits and approves.

**S5 ÔÇö Sprint Planning**

- Spec ÔåÆ dependency-aware task graph with estimates, owners, risk flags.
- Outcome-oriented roadmap (Now/Next/Later) synced automatically to Linear/Jira.

**S6 ÔÇö Agentic Build**

- In-product multi-file coding: Builder Agent claims file locks, checks out branches, and writes code.
- Surgical modifications across files, committing atomically and resolving conflict flags.

**S7 ÔÇö Visual QA**

- Sandbox preview environments generated automatically for visual validation of UI changes.
- Let designers and PMs audit layout and styling against design system tokens before merging.

**S8 ÔÇö Safe Release**

- Merges PRs, runs deploy checklists, deploys, and monitors production health.
- Automated rollback triggered if error metrics or exception counts spike post-deploy.

**S9 ÔÇö GTM Launch**

- Growth agent drafts release changelogs, marketing blog posts, newsletter copies, and announcement text.

**S10 ÔÇö Support Triage**

- Support agent triages incoming customer tickets, drafts answers, and routes bug logs back into Signal Capture (S1).

**S11 ÔÇö Cohort Analytics**

- Automated feature adoption tracking, cohort analysis, and outcome funnel monitoring.

**S12 ÔÇö Learn & Reflect**

- Outcome evaluation: compares performance telemetry with the original PRD spec.
- Updates the Product Memory Graph and publishes a learning brief to the portfolio dashboard.

### Cross-cutting platform (mandatory, spans all stages)

**X1 ÔÇö Orchestration & automation engine**

- Workflow definitions across stages; event/schedule/webhook triggers; an automation builder.
- **Many sub-agents running in parallel** within a mission; **many agent sessions running in parallel** across missions.
- A live orchestration view (the mission/agent graph) with per-node status, cost, and approval state.
- Planner/executor loop with max-step/max-cost caps, replay-and-branch, cancellation, checkpoints.

**X2 ÔÇö Multi-product & multi-workspace**

- **Multiple products in flight ÔÇö Product A/B/C ÔÇö grouped under Workspaces (A/B/C).**
- Per-product/workspace isolation of data, agents, memory, budgets, and access (RLS by `user_id` + `workspace_id`; see [`architecture/data.md`](./architecture/data.md)).
- Product switcher; cross-product portfolio view.

**X3 ÔÇö Trust & governance (the AI trust stack)**

- Per-call telemetry, LLM-as-judge scoring, guardrails (input + output), RAG with citations, prompt versioning + A/B, eval harness with regression gate, drift watch, budgets, live trace waterfall, incidents log, approval gates everywhere.

**X4 ÔÇö Product Memory**

- Queryable graph of signals ÔåÆ themes ÔåÆ opportunities ÔåÆ decisions ÔåÆ experiments ÔåÆ outcomes, with `supersedes` lineage; the institutional context agents reason over; exportable as skill packs.

**X5 ÔÇö Interop (agent-native)**

- MCP server (Cadence as a tool surface) + MCP client (consume external tools) + A2A (Agent Cards, delegate-to-agent, peer registry). Capability scopes, rate limits, prompt-injection guard on external results, audit log.

**X6 ÔÇö Identity, auth, billing**

- Auth (email + OAuth), session management, per-workspace membership (future: roles/teams), BYO model keys (encrypted), usage/billing metering against budgets. See [`architecture/security.md`](./architecture/security.md).

---

## 2. Granular feature catalog (login to agent-transfer, with what + why)

> **Sub-feature-level expansion:** [`docs/planning/feature-backlog.md`](./docs/planning/feature-backlog.md) takes every area below down to addressable sub-features with stable IDs, states, acceptance signals, dependencies, and a status ├ù build-order rollup. This section stays the narrative catalog; the backlog is the flat, ticket-ready list. Keep both true.

Every feature, grouped by area. Format: **Feature ÔÇö what it is ÔÇö _why we need it_.** This is the build checklist; each becomes an issue/spec. Status tags: `[reuse]` legacy survives, `[extend]` legacy base + new work, `[new]` build from scratch.

> **Inspiration, not comparison.** This catalog absorbs the best ideas from products worth learning from ÔÇö factory.ai's autonomous build/ship + live "mission" view (we extend it past code into launch/support), hyperagent's team-of-agents with per-agent budgets and self-improving memory, and Linear's agents-as-first-class-users + saved-workflow skills + event automations. We take the inspiration and build it into _our_ features below; we are not maintaining a competitor scorecard.

### A. Identity & access

- **Sign up / onboarding** ÔÇö email+password + Google OAuth; create first workspace + product; set display name, timezone, working hours. ÔÇö _Entry point; personalization and scheduling depend on it._ `[reuse]`
- **Login / logout** ÔÇö authenticated session, sign-out everywhere, session refresh, `Last-Event-ID` resume for streams. ÔÇö _Baseline security and reliable streaming._ `[reuse]`
- **Password reset / email verification** ÔÇö standard flows; verification on by default. ÔÇö _Account safety._ `[reuse]`
- **Profile & preferences** ÔÇö display name, role, timezone, working hours, default model per surface. ÔÇö _Drives greeting, scheduling, model routing._ `[reuse]`
- **BYO model keys** ÔÇö add/test/rotate/delete provider keys, encrypted; masked display. ÔÇö _Model-agnostic; cost control; enterprise trust._ `[reuse]`
- **Roles & membership (future)** ÔÇö invite, per-workspace roles, SSO/SAML. ÔÇö _Team and enterprise readiness._ `[new]`

### B. Workspaces & products

- **Create / switch workspace** ÔÇö top-level tenancy boundary. ÔÇö _Isolates a client/company/initiative._ `[extend]`
- **Create product under workspace** ÔÇö Product A/B/C inside a workspace; vision/problem/target-users/metrics/stage. ÔÇö _Run several products in parallel without bleed._ `[extend]`
- **Product switcher + portfolio view** ÔÇö fast switch; cross-product overview. ÔÇö _One operator, many products._ `[new]`
- **Per-product isolation** ÔÇö data, agents, memory, budgets scoped by `user_id`+`workspace_id`+product. ÔÇö _Security + correctness across products._ `[extend]`
- **Archive / delete product** ÔÇö lifecycle hygiene. ÔÇö _Avoid clutter; data governance._ `[new]`

### C. Agents ÔÇö configuration

- **Agent roster** ÔÇö list durable agents + spawned sub-agents per product. ÔÇö _See the team you command._ `[extend]`
- **Create / clone / configure agent** ÔÇö system prompt, tool allow-list, model, temperature/top*p/seed, max tokens, schedule, approval mode, memory toggle. ÔÇö \_Tailor behavior + governance per role.* `[reuse]`
- **Enable / disable / schedule agent** ÔÇö cron schedules with next-run preview. ÔÇö _Autonomy on a clock._ `[reuse]`
- **Agent detail + run history** ÔÇö last runs (status/duration/score/cost), memory inspector. ÔÇö _Trust through observability._ `[reuse]`

### D. Agent execution

- **Run on-demand / scheduled** ÔÇö manual trigger or cron fan-out. ÔÇö _Both reactive and proactive autonomy._ `[reuse]`
- **Planner/executor loop** ÔÇö plan ÔåÆ tool calls ÔåÆ observe ÔåÆ reflect ÔåÆ answer; max-step/max-cost caps. ÔÇö _Reliable multi-step autonomy._ `[reuse]`
- **Approval gates + Decision Queue** ÔÇö `auto|confirm|review`; queue of runs awaiting review; one-click resume from checkpoint. ÔÇö _Governed autonomy; the trust core._ `[reuse]`
- **Cancellation / replay-and-branch / checkpoints** ÔÇö stop mid-run (save partial), re-run against different model/prompt, resume. ÔÇö _Control + iteration._ `[reuse]`

### E. Agent communication, coordination & transfer (mandatory)

- **Sub-agent spawning** ÔÇö Orchestrator spawns ephemeral specialists per task. ÔÇö _Scale to the work without fixed seats._ `[new]`
- **Agent-to-agent messaging** ÔÇö structured internal A2A messages between agents in a mission. ÔÇö _Coordination without a human relaying context._ `[new]`
- **Agent transfer / handoff** ÔÇö pass a mission + its context, memory, and artifacts from one agent to another (e.g. Planner ÔåÆ Engineer ÔåÆ QA ÔåÆ Release). ÔÇö _Work flows across the lifecycle with zero context loss; this is the spine of the autonomous loop._ `[new]`
- **Parallel sub-agents** ÔÇö many specialists working a single mission concurrently. ÔÇö _Speed; mirrors a real team._ `[new]`
- **Parallel agent sessions** ÔÇö many missions running at once across products. ÔÇö _One operator, many things in flight._ `[new]`
- **Orchestration / mission graph view** ÔÇö live DAG of agents/sessions with per-node status, cost, approval state; pause/steer. ÔÇö _See and command the swarm._ `[new]`
- **Shared vs. private memory** ÔÇö mission-shared context + per-agent long-term memory with importance decay. ÔÇö _Coordination without leakage._ `[extend]`

### F. Discover

- **Signal ingest** ÔÇö paste/CSV now; connectors (Intercom/Zendesk/reviews/sales) next; sentiment on insert. ÔÇö _Raw material of discovery._ `[extend]`
- **Clustering ÔåÆ themes ÔåÆ opportunities** ÔÇö embed + cluster + synthesize with evidence ids; ICE scoring; dedupe by similarity. ÔÇö _Turn noise into ranked opportunities._ `[reuse]`
- **Continuous discovery feed** ÔÇö always-fresh per-product feed. ÔÇö _The lead use case; ongoing, not one-shot._ `[extend]`

### G. Define

- **PRD/spec generation** ÔÇö opportunity ÔåÆ structured cited draft. ÔÇö _Specs downstream of evidence, not vibes._ `[reuse]`
- **Doc editor + `/ai` + versions/diff** ÔÇö Tiptap, inline AI commands, autosave, version diff, citation pills. ÔÇö _Author + iterate with provenance._ `[reuse]`

### H. Plan

- **Task graph** ÔÇö spec ÔåÆ dependency-aware tasks with estimates/owners/risk. ÔÇö _Executable plan agents can run._ `[reuse]`
- **Outcome roadmap** ÔÇö Now/Next/Later; each item declares its outcome + measure. ÔÇö _Anti-feature-factory; ties work to results._ `[extend]`
- **Scheduling** ÔÇö agent proposes work blocks in working hours. ÔÇö _Time-aware execution._ `[reuse]`

### I. Build (autonomous)

- **Studio multi-file coding** ÔÇö agents write across files; per-hunk diff accept/reject; atomic revisions. ÔÇö _Agents build, not just suggest._ `[extend]`
- **Watch-the-agents-build surface** ÔÇö live per-session view: step, files, tool calls, cost, status; pause/steer/approve. ÔÇö _Trust + control over autonomous code._ `[new]`
- **Branch/worktree isolation per mission** ÔÇö each mission on its own branch. ÔÇö _Parallel safe building._ `[new]`

### J. Test (autonomous)

- **Test generation + run** ÔÇö agents author and run unit/integration/E2E + evals. ÔÇö _Quality without a human writing every test._ `[new]`
- **QA gate + self-correct loop** ÔÇö failing tests feed back to the build agent until green or escalate. ÔÇö _Closed-loop quality before ship._ `[new]`

### K. Ship

- **PR / deploy / release notes** ÔÇö open PRs, run deploy checklist, deploy, draft notes ÔÇö behind approval. ÔÇö _Autonomous delivery, governed._ `[new]`
- **Rollback triggers** ÔÇö documented per release. ÔÇö _Safe shipping._ `[new]`

### L. Launch / GTM / price

- **Launch + positioning + pricing + distribution drafts** ÔÇö agent-drafted, human-approved before external. ÔÇö _The lifecycle past code, that point tools skip._ `[new]`
- **Customer-facing pages / announcements** ÔÇö generated, approved. ÔÇö _Close the go-to-market gap._ `[new]`

### M. Operate / support

- **Ticket triage + draft answers + route/escalate** ÔÇö agents handle inbound; themes flow back to Discover. ÔÇö _Support closes the loop into discovery._ `[new]`

### N. Learn

- **Decisions + `supersedes`** ÔÇö outcomes write decisions with lineage. ÔÇö _Auditable "why," and belief updates._ `[reuse]`
- **Re-score + insight memo + daily brief** ÔÇö outcomes re-rank opportunities; memo surfaces in the brief. ÔÇö _The loop compounds._ `[extend]`

### O. Product Memory

- **Knowledge graph + query** ÔÇö signalsÔåÆdecisionsÔåÆoutcomes, typed nodes/edges. ÔÇö _Institutional context agents reason over._ `[new]`
- **Currency / drift on facts + skill packs** ÔÇö flag stale facts; export versioned skill bundles over MCP. ÔÇö _Memory stays true; reusable expertise._ `[new]`

### P. Trust & observability

- **Telemetry + traces + judge scores** ÔÇö per-call events, trace waterfall, LLM-as-judge. ÔÇö _Measure every AI action._ `[reuse]`
- **Guardrails + prompt studio + eval harness + drift + budgets + incidents** ÔÇö input/output guards, versioned prompts + A/B, regression-gated evals, drift watch, budget caps, incident log. ÔÇö _Make autonomy safe, improvable, affordable._ `[reuse]`
- **AI message contract** ÔÇö score/model/latency/tokens/cost/citations/feedback/trace/replay on every AI message. ÔÇö _Trust is the UI._ `[reuse]`

### Q. Interop (agent-native)

- **MCP server + client** ÔÇö expose Cadence as tools; consume external tools. ÔÇö _Be the place agents plug in._ `[new]`
- **A2A server/client + Agent Cards + scopes/limits/audit** ÔÇö peer agents, delegate-to-agent, governed. ÔÇö _Cross-vendor agent ecosystem._ `[new]`

### R. Platform & ops

- **Command palette (ÔîÿK) + global search** ÔÇö resolve every destination/action/artifact. ÔÇö _Keyboard-first speed._ `[reuse]`
- **Connectors / integrations** ÔÇö Docs, Notion, Linear, Calendar, GitHub, Slack, CRM. ÔÇö _Act on the systems the operator lives in._ `[extend]`
- **Notifications + budgets config + settings** ÔÇö approvals, breaches, guardrail rules, integration health. ÔÇö _Operate the platform._ `[extend]`

---

## 3. Build order (v4 milestones ÔÇö each independently demo-able)

> Canonical milestone definitions with proof bars: [`docs/strategy/v4-feature-map-2026-06-11.md`](./docs/strategy/v4-feature-map-2026-06-11.md) ┬º9. The foundation invariants (blast-radius limits, spend caps, kill-switch, prompt-injection defense, provider fallback, durable runtime, sandboxed execution ÔÇö see [`docs/planning/considerations.md`](docs/planning/considerations.md)) remain P0 architecture, already largely in place; every milestone below builds on them, never around them.

1. **M1 ÔÇö The Golden Path (demo-ready).** One continuous, watchable run: connect Slack/GitHub ÔåÆ Scout themes ÔåÆ Strategist ranks (Critic attached) ÔåÆ approve ÔåÆ Scribe cited spec ÔåÆ approve ÔåÆ Planner task graph ÔåÆ Builder PR + CI green ÔåÆ release-note draft ÔåÆ outcome card. Includes `F-IA-V4` (collapse 34 routes to the 7-surface IA), vocabulary enforcement, cost-per-mission chip, narrated empty states. _This fixes "not demo-ready" before anything new is added._
2. **M2 ÔÇö The Loop Closes (the differentiator).** The right half becomes real: support triage loop (LRN-01), analytics inbound (SEN-05), launch kits (LCH-01), outcome reviews (LRN-02), visible re-score (LRN-03), memory consult/write on every mission (ENG-05), cost-per-artifact (ENG-06). Proof: a support-ticket cluster re-ranks the opportunity queue with zero human transport.
3. **M3 ÔÇö The Team Arrives.** Roles + per-persona approval lanes (ENG-08), design scaffolds + handoff (DEF-04/05), visual validation (BLD-06), enablement notes (LCH-04), spec comments, multi-seat.
4. **M4 ÔÇö The Org Runs Itself.** Portfolio view, budget enforcement UX, MCP server/client + A2A delegate-out (ENG-07, BLD-04), skill packs (LRN-05), enterprise plane (ENG-09), pricing briefs (LCH-03).
5. **M5 ÔÇö Compounding.** Memory-graph querying as product surface, stale-fact drift, cross-product learnings, connector breadth, outcome-priced enterprise plans.

Sequencing rule unchanged: architecture first, so later stages are _additions, not rewrites_. See [`docs/decisions/tech-stack.md`](./docs/decisions/tech-stack.md).

---

## 4. Active build log (update as we ship)

### 2026-06-18

**D4-REPLAY (cycle 25) ┬À replay-and-branch (re-run a mission with a different model).** The cancel half of D4 shipped earlier; this adds replay-and-branch. The headline ("re-run with a different model") was mostly UI exposure: `startOrchestratedMission`/`StartSchema` already accepted `model` and threaded it to `runAgentLoop`, but the `retry` button never offered the choice. Generalized `retry` into a `replay` mutation with a **model picker + "Replay" button** in the mission header (shown for terminal non-failed missions; the failure panel keeps its contextual replay, default model). Added the **branch link**: migration `20260618160000_d4_replay_branch_link.sql` adds `missions.replayed_from_mission_id` (additive, idempotent, FK `ON DELETE SET NULL` so deleting an original never orphans/cascades) + a partial index; `StartSchema` gained `replayedFrom`, written to the new mission in a SEPARATE pre-migration-tolerant update right after `createMission` (so chat's mission path is untouched and the replay still runs if the column is absent); `getMission` resolves `replayed_from_mission_id` via a SEPARATE error-tolerant read (the main select and the whole detail page keep working before the migration applies); the new mission shows a "Replayed from an earlier mission" link to the parent. Replay re-plans from the goal via the orchestrator, so the model affects both planning and execution (A/B a goal across models). **Decision:** the rich side-by-side checkpoint-diff is deferred as D4b; the branch link is the lightweight diff affordance (open both). **Gate:** `tsc --noEmit` clean, `bun run build` green, `eslint` clean on the three touched files, humanization scan of additions clean, migration-safety hook passed. **Adversarial review:** no real fix (additive migration, tolerant set + read so pre-migration is safe, no redundant replay affordances between header + failure panel, model defaults to undefined when unset). Clean sync (no parallel commit). **Pending publish + live verify (migration + dispatch + UI).** **Files:** `src/lib/orchestrator.functions.ts`, `src/lib/missions.functions.ts`, `src/routes/_authenticated.missions.$missionId.tsx`, `supabase/migrations/20260618160000_d4_replay_branch_link.sql`, `docs/features/d4-mission-cancellation.md`, `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, `docs/planning/SOURCE-OF-TRUTH.md`, `docs/strategy/session-decisions.md`, `docs/planning/overnight-build-report.md`, this log.

**K2 (cycle 24) ┬À operator revert-to-revision (one-action rollback).** The Build engine recorded a revision per `studio.commit` (I1b) but had no way to roll back. K2 adds a confirm-gated "Revert" button on every prior revision in the Changes tab. New shared helper `src/lib/ai/studio-revert.server.ts` (`revertChangesetToRevision`) performs a NON-DESTRUCTIVE revert via the GitHub Git Data API: GET the target revision's commit tree, GET the current branch head, POST a new commit `{ tree: targetTree, parents: [headSha] }`, then PATCH the ref with `force:false`. History only moves forward (the revert is itself a normal, revertible commit) and a stale-parent race is refused by GitHub rather than clobbering work; the revert is recorded as the next revision. `revertToRevision` (server fn in `studio.functions.ts`) resolves GitHub auth for the changeset's workspace via `resolveGitHub` and delegates to the helper. The ChangesPanel button (`useConfirm`-gated) shows only while the branch is live (`committed`/`pr_open`) and never on the latest revision (a no-op). The helper is self-contained (its own gh fetch helpers, no `registry.server.ts` import) so a future `studio.revert` agent engine-tool can reuse it without a circular dependency. **No migration.** **Decision (operator-first):** shipped the operator door first because it needs no `agent_tools` migration, is self-authorizing (the human clicks), and is the literal "revert button" the spec names; the agent engine-tool (K2b) is deferred since the loop only exposes tools seeded in `agent_tools`. **Gate:** `tsc --noEmit` clean, `bun run build` green, `eslint` clean on all three touched files, humanization scan of additions clean. **Adversarial review:** no real fix (non-destructive by construction, revision lookup scoped to the changeset, GitHub commit applied before the best-effort revision record so a DB hiccup can't falsely report a failed revert, queries RLS-scoped). Clean sync (no parallel commit). **Pending publish + live verify (GitHub mutation + UI).** **Files:** new `src/lib/ai/studio-revert.server.ts`, `src/lib/studio.functions.ts`, `src/components/studio/ChangesPanel.tsx`, `docs/features/studio.md`, `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, `docs/planning/SOURCE-OF-TRUTH.md`, `docs/strategy/session-decisions.md`, `docs/planning/overnight-build-report.md`, this log.

**P4-GATE (cycle 23) ┬À eval-regression as a hard merge gate.** The Studio/Build merge tool `studio.pr.merge` was hard-gated only on CI (the J2 gate, `studio-ci.ts`). P4-GATE adds its quality-side twin so the BUILDÔåÆSHIP loop cannot ship code unattended while output quality is measurably regressing. New pure module `src/lib/ai/eval-gate.ts` (`evalRegressionReadiness` + `EVAL_REGRESSION_THRESHOLD_PTS = 10` + `SuiteScorePair`), mirroring `studio-ci.ts`: given the latest-vs-prior completed avg_score per suite (0-100), it blocks if any suite dropped ÔëÑ10 points, naming the worst. The merge tool (`registry.server.ts`) reads the user's completed `eval_runs` (latest two per suite, `.eq("user_id")` + `status='completed'` + non-null avg_score, ordered desc, capped at 80), fetches suite names, and throws `MergeBlocked` when not allowed, right after the existing CI gate, inside the same `if (!prJson.merged)` block. **Scale:** avg_score is 0-100 (confirmed via `20260614160000_p3_ki14_eval_score_0to100.sql`), so the threshold is 10 points on 0-100. **Semantics (J2-analogous):** evals run on a schedule (`eval-tick`), so the gate reads the already-measured trend and never triggers a run; it is read-only, degrades to allowed when no suite has two completed runs, and the operator can always merge from GitHub directly (the gate governs only the agent's tool). **No migration.** **Gate:** `tsc --noEmit` clean, `bun run build` green, `eslint` clean on both touched files, humanization scan of additions clean. **Adversarial review:** no real fix (0-100 scale correct, drop = prior minus latest is the correct direction, `Number()` coercion + the non-null DB filter make NaN/null safe, both queries explicitly user-scoped). Clean sync (no parallel commit this cycle). **Pending publish + live verify.** **Files:** new `src/lib/ai/eval-gate.ts`, `src/lib/ai/tools/registry.server.ts`, `docs/features/studio.md`, `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, `docs/planning/SOURCE-OF-TRUTH.md`, `docs/strategy/session-decisions.md`, `docs/planning/overnight-build-report.md`, this log.

**P5-ALERT (cycle 22) ┬À drift threshold ÔåÆ in-app Attention feed.** Drift was a passive watcher: the detector (`ai/drift.server.ts`) opens `drift_incidents` rows when a metric crosses the user's baseline, but they only showed on the `/drift` page. P5-ALERT surfaces them where the operator already looks: a 4th probe in `getNotifications` (`src/lib/notifications.functions.ts`) reads open `drift_incidents` (most-recent 6, over the existing `(user_id, status, detected_at)` index) and pushes them into the R3 Attention feed as severity-coded cards. Severity maps `critical` ÔåÆ warning, anything else ÔåÆ info (drift is a heads-up, never a human-decision "action"); the card names the drifted metric (latency / cost / token use / error rate / quality score, via a label map) with the signed `delta_pct` vs baseline + the surface and model, and links to `/drift`. **No migration** (live-derived from an existing table, same pattern as the approval/stall/budget probes), capped so a noisy week cannot flood the feed, degrades to no items on error. **No UI change needed:** both consumers (`NotificationsPanel`, `AttentionBell`) key off `severity`, not `kind`, so adding the `drift` kind to the union was enough. **Gate:** `tsc --noEmit` clean, `bun run build` green, `eslint` clean on the touched file, humanization scan of additions clean. **Adversarial review:** no real fix (numeric `delta_pct` coercion is `Number.isFinite`-guarded, severity safe-defaults to info, query is RLS-scoped + explicitly `.eq("user_id")`). Clean sync (no parallel/runaway commit this cycle). **Pending publish + live verify.** **Files:** `src/lib/notifications.functions.ts`, `docs/features/r3-notifications.md`, `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, `docs/planning/SOURCE-OF-TRUTH.md`, `docs/strategy/session-decisions.md`, `docs/planning/overnight-build-report.md`, this log.

**F-AGENTS-MENTIONABLE (cycle 21) ┬À composer @-picker + case-insensitive parse, feature completed.** The server half of this feature (parse `@agentslug` ÔåÆ pre-planned single-step `mission_steps` dispatch via `advanceMissionCore`; see the cycle-19-labeled entry below for the server design) was auto-committed mid-build by a parallel process (`40646dce0a` + report `ffbf5c50c0`) while the main loop was still working the same worktree, so the committed `chat.ts` already matched the main loop's server work. This cycle layered the genuinely-new value on top: (1) the **composer @-agent picker** in `_authenticated.chat.tsx`, a floating list above the composer (reuses `listAgents`, filtered to enabled non-orchestrator agents) with arrow-key nav + Enter/Tab/click to insert `@slug `; the picker drives those keys ONLY while open, so the Enter-to-send path is byte-identical when it is closed and can never be hijacked; placeholder + helper line advertise the affordance; (2) a **case-insensitive parse fix** in `chat.ts` (`parseAgentMentions` `/gi` + lowercased candidate, `stripMention` `i` flag) so a manually-typed `@Strategist` resolves to the lowercase `strategist` slug, matching the composer's already-case-insensitive `detectMentionQuery`. **Why single-step DAG (not "just run the agent"):** `maybeCompleteMission` keys off `steps.length > 0`; a mission with zero steps and no orchestrator run hangs at `running` forever, so the mention pre-plans one step and lets the deterministic `advanceMissionCore` cron dispatch + finalize it (cheaper + faster than the orchestrator path, exact agent honored). **Gate:** `tsc --noEmit` clean, `bun run build` green, `eslint` clean on both touched files, humanization scan of additions clean (zero em/en dashes). **Adversarial review folded one real fix:** the server parse was case-sensitive while the composer was not, so a typed `@Strategist` would silently miss; made both case-insensitive. **Process note (recurring):** a background process is committing/pushing autonomously again (same pattern as the F3 `c304bf6396` incident); logged in `session-decisions.md`. **Pending publish + live verify.** **Files:** `src/routes/_authenticated.chat.tsx` (composer @-picker), `src/routes/api/chat.ts` (case-insensitive parse), `docs/features/agents-mentionable.md` (new), `docs/features/README.md`, `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, `docs/planning/SOURCE-OF-TRUTH.md`, `docs/strategy/session-decisions.md`, `docs/planning/overnight-build-report.md`, this log.

**F3-CRON (cycle 20) ┬À continuous auto-cluster, built gated-off, verified + closed.** The auto-cluster cron deferred at cycles 11/17 (recurring AI spend = founder-gated) is now BUILT in the autonomous-safe shape: shipped off by default so applying it commits zero spend, with the recurring-spend scheduler left as the one founder activation step. Extracted the LLM clustering body into a shared core `clusterSignalsCore` (`src/lib/ai/cluster.server.ts`) called by both the user-triggered `clusterSignals` and a new `cluster-tick` hook (`src/routes/api/public/hooks/cluster-tick.ts`); the core explicitly filters `signals.user_id` so the service-role cron path (RLS off) clusters one owner at a time (never across users), passes `workspaceId` so the kill-switch + budget caps still govern spend, and stamps `themes.workspace_id` explicitly (the cron has no `auth.uid()` for the DB default). Owner-gated `getWorkspaceClusterSettings` / `toggleAutoCluster` server fns back a "Auto-cluster new signals" toggle in `SignalsPanel.tsx` (owner-only, shows last-run time). Migration `20260618140000_f3_auto_cluster.sql` adds `workspaces.auto_cluster_enabled` (NOT NULL DEFAULT false) + `last_auto_cluster_at` + a partial index for the cron query; additive, idempotent, zero spend on apply. The cron is batch-capped at 5 workspaces (oldest-run-first) and tolerates the pre-migration window (`42703`/`PGRST204` soft-pass). **Adversarial review (prior session) caught + fixed a service-role `workspace_id` NOT-NULL bug.** **Gate (this turn):** `tsc --noEmit` clean, `bun run build` green (the `cluster-tick` route bundles), `eslint` clean on all four touched files, F3 source + migration scan zero em/en dashes. **Activation (founder, section 4 of the SSOT):** apply the migration on publish, owners enable the toggle, then point pg_cron at the hook (snippet in the migration header). **Pending publish + live verify.** **Files:** new `src/lib/ai/cluster.server.ts`, `src/routes/api/public/hooks/cluster-tick.ts`, `supabase/migrations/20260618140000_f3_auto_cluster.sql`; edited `src/lib/discovery.functions.ts`, `src/components/product/SignalsPanel.tsx`, generated `src/integrations/supabase/types.ts` + `src/routeTree.gen.ts`; `docs/features/f3-continuous-discovery.md`, `docs/planning/SOURCE-OF-TRUTH.md`, this log.

**O1 (cycle 19) ┬À provenance in the shared Lineage drawer ÔÇö gate-green, pending publish.** Extended the O1 provenance slice (root-signal trace) from the two drill surfaces (opportunity, spec/PRD) to the cross-cutting `LineageDrawer`, so "why does this exist?" is answerable wherever lineage opens, not only on two detail pages. A new "Traces back to" section sits below the existing "Came from" parents and reuses `getProvenance` (no new server fn, no migration). It is shown only when the chain is deeper than one hop (`signal_count > 0 && depth > 1`), so it never just duplicates "Came from" for a theme (whose immediate parents already are signals). **Adversarial review folded one fix:** the section listed `source_signals.slice(0, 8)` while the header printed the full `signal_count`, so a deep artifact (>8 root signals) silently dropped the rest; added a "+N more source signals" overflow line so the visible list and the count agree. **Decision:** this was uncommitted in-progress work recovered from the prior session's mid-build rollover; verified sound (field contracts + the `signal` route all check out) and finished rather than discarded. **Verification:** `tsc --noEmit` 0 errors, `eslint` clean, `prettier` clean, `bun run build` green, humanization scan clean. **Files:** `src/components/cadence/LineageDrawer.tsx`, `docs/features/o1-provenance.md`, `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, `docs/planning/overnight-build-report.md`, this log.

**RULE ┬À data minimalism ("every field earns its place") + onboarding `role` removed ÔÇö landed on `main`.** Founder principle, made a standing convention: we capture nothing by default; no field, input, stored column, or pixel of screen real estate exists unless a _named consumer_ needs it (now, or with a documented credible near-term use), and a captured field ships in the same change as its consumer (no "collect now, use later"). Unearned capture costs the user's time, our storage, privacy surface, and maintenance, forever. **Applied immediately:** an audit of `profiles.role` found it is never mapped to anything ÔÇö no roleÔåÆagent config, settings, or gating; its only "use" was being incidentally swept into the chat-grounding JSON blob. The persona that actually customizes the workspace is the onboarding track selector, not a free-text role. So `role` was removed from `BasicDetailsStep` (name only now); it returns only when wired to a real consumer (e.g. role-based personalization). **What shipped:** new convention [`docs/conventions/data-minimalism.md`](./docs/conventions/data-minimalism.md) (the Value Test + the wiring rule + the narrow future-use clause + the `role` worked example), indexed in the conventions README, wired into [`AGENTS.md`](./AGENTS.md) ┬º3.0b (sibling to the Engine-Room Doctrine) + a ┬º5 trigger row ("adding a captured field ÔåÆ run the Value Test first"); `BasicDetailsStep.tsx` role field + state + write removed (docstring explains the name-only-by-design choice). **Verification:** `tsc --noEmit` 0 errors, `eslint` clean, `bun run build` green. **Files:** `docs/conventions/data-minimalism.md` new, `docs/conventions/README.md`, `AGENTS.md` (┬º3.0b + ┬º5), `src/components/onboarding/BasicDetailsStep.tsx`, this log.

**ONBOARDING ┬À basic-details step + credentials-only signup (fixes the OAuth `abc.def` name) ÔÇö shipped on `main` (no migration).** Founder report: a Google signup had no name, so the whole app addressed the user by the email local-part (`abc.def`). Root cause: identity capture was asymmetric ÔÇö email/password grabbed name inline at `/signup`, the Google path captured nothing and the `handle_new_user` trigger only ever set `full_name` (never `display_name`), so both greeting surfaces fell back to `email.split("@")[0]`. **Decision (founder deferred the call):** adopt the industry-standard split (Linear/Notion/Vercel) ÔÇö authenticate first, capture profile second, prefilled from the OAuth provider ÔÇö rather than keep name on the signup form for one path only. **What shipped:** (1) new `src/components/onboarding/BasicDetailsStep.tsx` ÔÇö first/last name + role, the single identity-capture surface for BOTH signup paths; rendered as the first gate in `OnboardingFlow` only when the profile lacks a `display_name`; prefills from auth `user_metadata` (`given_name`/`family_name`/`full_name`) for Google, blank for bare email, and NEVER seeds from the email local-part; on submit writes BOTH `profiles` (via `updateProfile`) AND auth `user_metadata` (via `supabase.auth.updateUser`) because Today reads the profiles row while the AppShell chip + chat header read the session metadata ÔÇö fixing one without the other leaves the wrong name on the other surface. (2) `/signup` reduced to credentials only (email + password + Google); name/role inputs removed; profile upsert now `{ onboarded: false }` so the gate routes into onboarding where the details step runs. (3) Fixed a pre-existing humanized-output violation (em-dash in the password placeholder). **Engine-Room:** none (calm-front identity capture). **Verification:** `tsc --noEmit` 0 errors, `eslint` clean, `bun run build` green, and both screens visually verified on-brand via a throwaway preview route + Playwright at 1440px (Ember Editorial: parchment, ember reserved for the single CTA, serif italic-em title, mono-label kicker; preview route reverted before commit). Live walkthrough (fresh Google signup ÔåÆ name prefilled ÔåÆ setup) confirms on the next publish. **Files:** `src/components/onboarding/BasicDetailsStep.tsx` new, `src/components/onboarding/OnboardingFlow.tsx`, `src/routes/signup.tsx`, `docs/features/auth-flows.md`, `docs/features/onboarding-tracks.md`, this log.

**HOTFIX ┬À onboarding track-pick crashed every new user with an RLS error ÔÇö fixed on `main` (no migration).** The published demo blocked at "Setup ┬À Step 1 of 4": clicking any track (Solo PM / Founding PM / Tech Founder) raised **"new row violates row-level security policy for table 'projects'"**, and the user could not enter the app. **Root cause (systematic-debugging, traced through the migrations):** `seedWorkspaceForTrack` inserts into `projects` / `signals` / `opportunities` without setting `workspace_id`, trusting the `current_user_default_workspace()` column default added in the tenancy retrofit (`20260530120200_tenancy_c`). That migration also swapped those tables' write RLS from `auth.uid() = user_id` to **membership-keyed** `is_workspace_member(workspace_id)`. The default resolves to the caller's earliest `workspace_members` row ÔÇö but a brand-new user reaches onboarding (their first write) before that row reliably exists: `handle_new_user()` calls `ensure_default_workspace()` inside a swallow-all `EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS` block, that function isn't in our migrations (Lovable-managed, drift-prone, and the KI-13 saga shows the trigger body keeps getting reverted), and demo accounts skip the provisioning entirely. No membership ÔåÆ `is_workspace_member(NULL)` is false ÔåÆ the `projects` INSERT is rejected. Every track button fails identically because they all hit the same insert. **Fix:** made onboarding self-healing. New `ensureDefaultWorkspace(supabase, userId)` helper in `onboarding.functions.ts` resolves the default workspace via the RPC, else reuses an owned-but-unmembered workspace, else creates `workspaces {owner_id, name}` + the owner `workspace_members` row (all permitted to the user-scoped client by the `ws owner manage` / `owner manages members` policies); `seedWorkspaceForTrack` calls it first and sets `workspace_id` **explicitly** on all three inserts ÔÇö the path migration C documented as intended ("set workspace_id explicitly in server functions"). Defense-in-depth: onboarding can no longer fail this way even after signup provisioning is repaired. **Why a server-function fix, not a migration:** it ships on the next Lovable publish with no migration-sync gate (the exact gate that keeps reverting `handle_new_user`). **Verification:** `tsc --noEmit` 0 errors (the real gate), `eslint` clean, `prettier` clean, `bun run build` green. Live proof requires a fresh non-demo signup ÔåÆ pick a track after republish (could not reproduce locally ÔÇö Supabase MCP unauthenticated this session). **Standing follow-up:** the deeper signup-provisioning fragility (`ensure_default_workspace` absent from repo migrations + swallowed in the trigger) remains a known issue ÔÇö see `docs/planning/known-issues.md`. **Files:** `src/lib/onboarding.functions.ts`, `docs/features/onboarding-tracks.md`, `docs/planning/known-issues.md`, this log.

**Onboarding ┬À first-run gate fix + 4-step redesign ÔÇö shipped on `main`.** The founder published W6 and signed up with Google: onboarding never appeared, landing straight on Home. **Root cause:** the first-run gate (`_authenticated.tsx` + `onboarding-gate.ts`) redirects only on `profiles.onboarded === false`, but the only path that reliably wrote that flag was the email/password client-side upsert in `signup.tsx`; the Google (Lovable OAuth) path has no such write and leans on the unreliable `handle_new_user` trigger (KI-13), whose resilient body swallows a failed profile insert. So an OAuth signup had no profile row, and the gate's "missing row counts as onboarded" fail-open rule sent them past onboarding. **Fix:** the gate now treats a missing row as a brand-new account, upserts `{ onboarded: false }` (ignoreDuplicates, never clobbers an existing row) and routes into first-run, making the gate the single source of truth for every signup path (`82281c21c3`). **Redesign** (founder: "UI/UX looks crap, no value"): built in an isolated `git worktree` (a parallel session was actively resetting the main tree and had already wiped the uncommitted fix once) with `impeccable` (onboard) + `emil-design-eng` against the Ember Editorial canon; all 4 steps rendered + screenshotted via a throwaway preview harness (reverted before merge). Step 1 `TrackSelector` now names the outcome ÔÇö each persona card previews the real workspace + first teardown it delivers, read from the seed data ÔÇö instead of "we'll seed sample data"; steps 2-4 get serif italic-em titles (`listen` / `staff` / `goal`), value copy that names the outcome, and the user-facing em-dashes removed (humanized-output); ember reserved for the single CTA; staggered transform-only entrance + `.lift` press feedback, reduced-motion gated (`40a0f51a5b`, `00a051a1c3`). Logic, mutations, and the founder skip-as-primary ruling unchanged. **Verification:** `tsc` / `eslint` / `prettier` / `bun run build` all green; the OAuth round-trip is verifiable only on the next publish. **Files:** `src/lib/onboarding-gate.ts`, `src/components/onboarding/TrackSelector.tsx`, `src/components/onboarding/OnboardingFlow.tsx`, `docs/features/onboarding-tracks.md`, `docs/features/README.md` (W6 index row), `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, this log.

**MOAT-METRIC ┬À outcome-accuracy on the Gauntlet ÔÇö built + tsc/lint/build-verified on `main` workflow.** The moat made measurable (Lane B, the founder's "build next" pick). Adds a fifth Gauntlet card, **Outcome accuracy**: of the bets you shipped and then reviewed, the share that VALIDATED, with a trend (is it climbing as the loop's memory compounds?). **DEC-02-LOOP ┬À the Critic promoted to a routable agent-loop tool ÔÇö built + tsc/build-verified on `main`.** Closes the v10 M-B "Critic as an explicit loop step" item with the _safe_ increment (recon blueprint from a 3-reader engine map): make the Critic a registered, agent-callable tool WITHOUT touching the fragile mission-DAG machinery. (3) Today's "What changed" card now **names the moved opportunity** instead of "a priority" (the data flows for free from the enriched fn). **A real type trap was caught and fixed before it shipped:** my first cut typed the flattened row with an index signature (`[k: string]: unknown`), which would have weakened `latestRescore.verdict` to `unknown` and broken Today's JSX (`{latestRescore.verdict}` is not a valid `ReactNode`) ÔÇö the original returned `any` so it had compiled; replaced with a precise `LearningWire` type, and `tsc` then confirmed Today renders. **Coordination:** built on the LEARN lane, file-disjoint from WEDGE; the working tree arrived with an **accidental deletion of the committed `WedgeTeardown.tsx`** (WEDGE lane) that broke the whole build (`tsc` error: cannot find the module the committed Today route imports) ÔÇö restored it from `HEAD` (returns the tree to committed truth; **WEDGE ┬À Critic-teardown first-run (the v10 launch wedge, P0 #2) ÔÇö SHIPPED to `main`.** Picked the next item in the v10 pick-order after LRN-02. **Recon first (background Explore agent) confirmed the wedge is pure integration, not new capability:** the Critic engine (`runCritic`, DEC-02), the `opportunities` table (`critic_review jsonb`), and the `VerdictChip`/`CriticBadge` renderers already exist, so there is **no new AI infra and no migration** ÔÇö the work is intake + surface. Built two pieces in lockstep: (1) a server fn `runWedgeTeardown({ idea, problem?, target_user?, project_id? })` in `discovery.functions.ts` that records the idea as an opportunity **verbatim** (neutral ICE 5/5/5 ÔÇö we don't fake a score the operator didn't give; `missing_evidence` carries most of the first-run value) scoped to the active product, then calls the module-private `runCritic({kind:"opportunity"})` inline, returning `{ opportunity, review }`; and (2) `WedgeTeardown.tsx`, a self-contained formÔåÆresult surface that leads the **cold-start** "Start here" section on Today (above the existing signal on-ramp), reusing the `VerdictChip` tones. Fixed two ways: the component holds the result in local state and does **not** invalidate `["cold-start"]`, and the cold-start query now sets `refetchOnWindowFocus: false` + `refetchOnReconnect: false` so it only re-evaluates on a genuine remount. Also handled the no-AI-key path honestly (`review` can be `null` ÔåÆ "Saved, the Critic could not run" fallback, not a broken card), and swapped smart quotes for straight quotes in the one user-facing title line (humanized-output gate). **Verification: `bunx tsc --noEmit` 0 errors (the real type gate ÔÇö `bun run build` strips types without checking); `bun run lint` shows zero problems in the three changed files.** Full end-to-end (the real cited verdict) needs the deployed app ÔÇö local dev has no AI key, and cold-start needs an empty workspace. **LRN-02 ┬À Outcome reviews ÔÇö Historian verdict (predicted vs actual) ÔÇö SHIPPED to `main`.** Picked the v10 P0 #1 (`LRN-02` + `W1-AUTO`, the "close the loop / moat" item). **Recon first saved a rebuild:** the core was already built and the dashboard status was stale ÔÇö `recordOutcome` already takes a human verdict, re-scores the linked opportunity's ICE, writes a `learnings` row, and (W1-AUTO) calls `rememberOutcome`, which embeds the outcome into a recallable global `agent_memory` row so future runs compound it. So W1-AUTO is done/wired (marked Ô£à with evidence), and only the genuine gap vs v10's wording ("predicted vs actual, **Historian verdict**") remained: the verdict was entered **purely manually**. Built that: a new `suggestOutcomeVerdict({prdId, metricLabel?, metricValue?, notes?})` server fn assembles the **prediction** (the opportunity's problem / hypothesis / predicted ICE, plus ÔÇö once the H2 sync lands ÔÇö its committed roadmap outcome + measure; read via `select("*")` so it's pre-migration tolerant) and the **actual** signal so far (metric + operator notes), then calls the AI chokepoint (reusing `surface:"judge"` so it needs no edit to the shared `runtime.server.ts` ÔÇö collision-free with the parallel engine lane) for strict JSON `{predicted, verdict, summary}`, enum-clamps the verdict (validated/missed/mixed, default mixed), and returns it. On the `OutcomeCard`, a "Draft with Historian" button pre-fills the verdict + summary and shows a "Predicted:" line; the human still confirms and fires the unchanged `recordOutcome`, so the rescore + memory write stay human-gated. The whole thing only DRAFTS ÔÇö no autonomous write. **Adversarial review (ecc:code-reviewer): APPROVE, 0 HIGH;** folded 1 MED (clear the stale `predicted` line via `onMutate` on a re-draft) + 1 LOW (dropped a no-op `fallbackModel` equal to the primary). Prompt-injection risk assessed LOW (user's own workspace data + enum-clamped output + human-confirm gate). **Verification: `bunx tsc --noEmit` 0 errors, `bunx eslint` clean, `bun run build` green.** **Files:** `src/lib/outcome.functions.ts` (`suggestOutcomeVerdict`), `src/components/product/OutcomeCard.tsx`; `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, this log. **OPS-01 audio ┬À real ElevenLabs soundscapes generated (experimental free-tier set).** Connected the ElevenLabs MCP and generated the Flow-mode ambient tracks into `public/soundscape/`. Final set (all ElevenLabs **Sound Effects**, 5s, looped, ~80KB each): **Ocean ┬À Monsoon (rain + temple bells) ┬À Bansuri (flute texture) ┬À Forest (Himalayan) ┬À Heartbeat (bass-rich ~75bpm) ┬À Fireplace**; default is Ocean. Two iterations with the founder: the first cut included **Tanpura** and **Singing bowls**, both removed as too harsh; root cause documented (a 5s SFX loop repeats a transient _attack_ like a pluck/strike every 5s, so it "hits", whereas continuous textures like water, fire, rain, and forest loop invisibly), and the heartbeat was regenerated bassier/punchier. The **Music API (`compose_music`) is paid-only** (free tier returns 402), so real melodic/cultural music (lo-fi raga, a full bansuri melody, Balinese gamelan, a smooth long tanpura) is **deferred with a full pick-up plan + exact prompts** in `public/soundscape/README.md` (the "TODO when on a paid plan" + "Tried and rejected" sections). Presets renamed across `session.ts` / `FlowWidget.tsx` / `use-flow-mode.tsx` (+ test); the audio engine, dim, timer, custom-length, and notification-quieting are unchanged. **License note:** these are committed as an _experimental_ free-tier set (generally non-commercial); confirm commercial terms before treating as production assets (gate recorded in the README table). **Verification:** 21 `bun test` green, `tsc --noEmit` 0 errors, `eslint` clean (one pre-existing react-refresh warning). **Files:** `public/soundscape/*.mp3` (6) + `README.md` new; `src/lib/flow/{session.ts,soundscape.ts}` (+`session.test.ts`), `src/components/cadence/FlowWidget.tsx`, `src/hooks/use-flow-mode.tsx`, `docs/features/flow-mode.md`, this log.

**B5 ┬À Product lifecycle (archive / restore / export / delete) ÔÇö SHIPPED to `main`.** Built the full product lifecycle onto the `/product` **Portfolio** (the continuation of B3), extracting the inline portfolio into `src/components/product/PortfolioBoard.tsx`. Four per-product actions: **soft archive + restore** (reversible ÔÇö an Undo toast, and a durable Archived section to restore from; archived products drop out of the sidebar + product tabs), **JSON export** of the product's whole footprint (project + signals + opportunities + specs + tasks ÔÇö the escape hatch / U6-lite), and an **honest export-then-delete**. The delete follows the destructive-actions doctrine: `useConfirm({ destructive, typedConfirm: name })` (type the exact product name) with **honest copy** ÔÇö because the FK is `on delete set null`, deleting a product _detaches_ its signals/opps/specs/tasks to the workspace rather than destroying them (the old AppShell sidebar delete's "everything inside it" copy was factually wrong); a JSON snapshot auto-downloads first as the safety net. **Server (`projects.functions.ts`):** new `setProjectArchived({id, archive})` (verified write ÔÇö `.eq("user_id").select("id")`, throws on 0 rows), `exportProduct({id})` (RLS-scoped reads), hardened `deleteProject` (now a verified delete, not a phantom-ok bare delete); `listProjects` JS-filters archived out (pre-migration tolerant ÔÇö no SQL reference to the not-yet-existing column) and `getPortfolio`/`PortfolioProduct` gained an `archived` flag. **Migration** `20260617120000_b5_project_archive.sql` adds `archived_at` + a partial index `WHERE archived_at IS NULL`; the existing "own projects all" RLS (FOR ALL on user_id) already scopes it. **Adversarial review (ecc:code-reviewer) caught a real HIGH:** `useConfirm()` returns the confirm fn directly (AppShell does `const confirm = useConfirm()`), so my `const { confirm } = useConfirm()` yielded `undefined` and would have thrown on every delete at runtime ÔÇö **and the Vite build never caught it because esbuild strips types without checking.** Folded that + two LOWs (verified delete, partial index), and a separate `tsc`-only error the source review couldn't see: the TanStack server-fn boundary rejects a `Record<string, unknown>` return as non-serializable, so `ProductExport` now uses a recursive JSON-safe type. **Verification: `bunx tsc --noEmit` 0 errors (the real type gate ÔÇö `bun run build` alone is not), `bunx eslint` clean, `bun run build` green.** Collision-free from the parallel engine lane (owns AppShell, which keeps only its bare sidebar delete). **Files:** `src/components/product/PortfolioBoard.tsx`, `supabase/migrations/20260617120000_b5_project_archive.sql` new; `src/lib/projects.functions.ts`, `src/routes/_authenticated.product.tsx` edited; `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, this log.

**H2 ┬À Outcome roadmap (Now/Next/Later) ÔÇö SHIPPED to `main`.** Built the outcome/commitment layer over the agent-ranked opportunities, as a **Roadmap tab on `/product`** (`?tab=roadmap`). This is explicitly NOT the task/sprint kanban that v6 deleted: the human _commits_ an opportunity to a Now/Next/Later bucket and declares an **outcome** (what changes) + a **measure** (how we know), and the agent's continuous ICE ranking orders the cards _within_ each bucket. Reconciled the v6 `/roadmap` deletion this way (outcome curation, not manual sequencing) rather than reviving the kanban. **Build:** a four-column board (Backlog ┬À Now ┬À Next ┬À Later) with native HTML5 drag (no `@dnd-kit` ÔÇö that dep isn't installed and the supply-chain guard would block adding it), optimistic move (onMutate snapshot ÔåÆ onError rollback ÔåÆ onSettled invalidate), and inline outcome/measure edit per card. **Data:** new `roadmap.functions.ts` ÔÇö `getRoadmap` reads `select("*")` so it is **pre-migration tolerant** (until the next Lovable sync adds the columns, every opportunity reads as unplaced and sits in the backlog; reads never error), and `updateRoadmapItem` patches the three roadmap columns. Migration `20260617000000_h2_roadmap_outcome.sql` adds `roadmap_bucket` (CHECK now/next/later) + `roadmap_outcome` + `roadmap_measure` to `opportunities`, idempotent, with a partial index on committed items; the existing "own opportunities all" RLS policy (FOR ALL on user*id) already scopes the new columns, so no new policy. **Adversarial review (3 fixes folded):** (1) the write now does `.eq("user_id", ÔÇª).select("id")` and throws if zero rows return, so an RLS-blocked or no-match update fails loudly instead of returning a phantom `ok:true` that would leave the optimistic UI lying; (2) added a keyboard/click bucket `<select>` per card (aria-labeled) so bucket-moves aren't drag-only (a11y); (3) the inline edit now resets its outcome/measure fields on save so a stale value can't leak into the next card opened. **Gate:** the place-into-bucket \_write* needs the migration, so it activates on the next Lovable sync; the board reads and renders today (everything in backlog). **Verification:** `bun run build` green, `bunx eslint` clean on all three files. Built collision-free from the parallel engine lane (`/product` + new files only; no AppShell/CommandPalette/Govern). **Files:** `supabase/migrations/20260617000000_h2_roadmap_outcome.sql`, `src/lib/roadmap.functions.ts`, `src/components/product/RoadmapBoard.tsx` new; `src/routes/_authenticated.product.tsx` (Roadmap tab wiring); `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, this log.

**OPS-01 follow-up ┬À Flow audio reworked from synthesis to real recordings + a custom timer (founder feedback).** The founder tested the shipped Flow mode and found all three synthesized presets (Rain/Wind/Deep, filtered white noise) harsh, which defeats a calm-focus feature. Reworked the audio engine: `src/lib/flow/soundscape.ts` is now a real-audio buffer player that fetches one looped recording per preset, decodes it once, loops it gaplessly via Web Audio (an HTMLAudioElement loop seams audibly), and crossfades on preset change with volume on a master gain. New presets are Rain/Ocean/Forest/Lo-fi/Heartbeat. The files live in `public/soundscape/<preset>.mp3` and are sourced separately, because I could not autonomously fetch great, no-attribution, loopable, license-clear audio (Pixabay is gated/403; Wikimedia Commons quality was poor and attribution-encumbered) and cannot audition for quality, so committing scraped audio would be a legal + quality risk. `start()` now resolves a boolean; when a file is absent the preset shows "This sound has no track yet" and stays silent while the rest of Flow mode (dim, timer, quieting) still works. Also added the requested **custom focus length**: a clamped minutes field (1 to 240) beside the 25/50/90/Open chips. `public/soundscape/README.md` documents the exact filenames, royalty-free/CC0 sources, and a per-file license-provenance table. **Verification:** 21 `bun test` green (+4 new: `presetSrc`, `clampMinutes`), `tsc --noEmit` clean, `eslint` clean (same pre-existing provider+hook react-refresh warning), humanization gate clean, dev server serves `/` 200 with no errors. **Decision:** logged in `session-decisions.md` (reverses the original "synthesized in-browser" OPS-01 choice). **Files:** `src/lib/flow/{soundscape.ts,session.ts}` (+`session.test.ts`), `src/hooks/use-flow-mode.tsx`, `src/components/cadence/FlowWidget.tsx`, `public/soundscape/README.md` new; `docs/features/flow-mode.md`, `docs/strategy/session-decisions.md`, this log.

A guarded sweep swapped ~171 brand references across ~40 files (the capitalized brand token plus two HTTP user-agent strings; `git mv` of the v3 positioning file to `v3-positioning-cadence-2026-06-10.md`), while genuine engineering terms (the cache fall-through and provider-resilience patterns) were deliberately protected by swapping only the capitalized brand form. ### 2026-06-16

**OPS-01 ┬À Flow mode (ambient calm-state) ÔÇö SHIPPED.** A one-click calm operating stance, living in the `AppShell` sidebar footer beside the theme toggle (chrome, not Today ÔÇö it's a global stance, so the home-and-today IA rubric puts it in the chrome). Turning it on dims the sidebar + TopBar (`html.flow`, lifting on hover; main content stays full), plays a synthesized ambient soundscape (Web Audio, no audio files: Rain/Wind/Deep presets are filtered looping noise with a slow LFO, + volume), runs a focus timer (25/50/90/open) that chimes and auto-exits at zero, and **quiets non-urgent notifications**. Quieting is the one structural piece: a `lib/notify.ts` facade re-exports `toast` with sonner's exact API, so a mechanical one-line import swap across **44 files** (`sonner` ÔåÆ `@/lib/notify`) routes every toast through it; while flow is on, success/info/message/default toasts are held in a buffer and replayed as one summary line on exit (`While you were focused ┬À N updates`), while errors/warnings (and anything `{critical:true}`) always pass through. State mirrors `use-theme.tsx` (context + `localStorage` + a documentElement class); no server table. A session resumes across reload (audio re-arms on a tap, per the browser autoplay policy). Engine-Room stamp recorded in the spec. Decisions were founder-chosen in planning: ambient calm-state (not a full-screen room), hold-then-summarize (not silent-suppress), synthesized audio (not bundled files). **Verification:** 163 `bun test` green (+17 new: notify facade + pure session/timer helpers), `tsc --noEmit` clean, `eslint` clean (one pre-existing provider+hook react-refresh warning, same as `use-theme`), humanization gate clean (0 dashes/invisible/buzzwords), dev server boots and serves `/` + `/login` 200 with no import errors. The ESLint regression-guard (ban `toast` from `sonner`) was blocked by the config-protection hook, so the convention is documented in the spec instead. **Files:** `src/lib/notify.ts` (+`.test.ts`), `src/lib/flow/{session.ts,soundscape.ts,chime.ts}` (+`session.test.ts`), `src/hooks/use-flow-mode.tsx`, `src/components/cadence/FlowWidget.tsx` new; `src/routes/_authenticated.tsx` (provider), `src/components/cadence/AppShell.tsx` (footer), `src/styles.css` (`html.flow` + `flowBreathe`), 44 files import-swapped; `docs/features/flow-mode.md` (+ index), `docs/planning/feature-dashboard.md`, `docs/conventions/home-and-today-ia.md`, this log.

**G3 engine lane ÔÇö adversarial review + 4 fixes (closeout).** Ran an `ecc:typescript-reviewer` correctness+security pass over the riskiest pieces (J2 merge gate, K1 release notes, I1 hunk apply). Fixed: **(HIGH/J2)** the CI gate fetched check-runs at `per_page=50` with no pagination, so a failing check beyond #50 (common in matrix builds) could read as green and let a red PR merge ÔÇö the dangerous false-allow direction; now `per_page=100` plus a fail-safe block when `total_count` exceeds the page (refuses rather than risks a false allow). **(HIGH/J2)** a closed-but-unmerged PR fell through to the GitHub merge call and returned a misleading "conflicts or pending checks" 405; now a clear `state != "open"` guard throws first. **(MED/I1)** stale hunk-ids from the UI under a concurrent edit could silently corrupt staged content (positional ids shift if `new_content` changed); added optimistic concurrency ÔÇö the UI passes the row's `updated_at` as `expectedUpdatedAt` and the server's UPDATE is conditional on it, returning a refresh-and-retry conflict instead of writing wrong content. **(MED/K1)** uncapped `studio_changeset_revisions.message` text flowed verbatim into the release-notes prompt (injection surface); each commit message is now capped to 500 chars (matching the work-order cap). The reviewer confirmed the rest correct: `overallFromChecks` priority ordering, `mergeReadinessFromCi` exhaustiveness, the `!merged` guard + gate placement outside `withIdempotency`, `applyHunkSelection` round-trips, the status='staged' guards, and K1 RLS tenancy. `bun test` 146 green, `bun run build` green. **Files:** `src/lib/ai/tools/registry.server.ts` (J2 gate), `src/lib/studio.functions.ts` (K1 cap + I1 concurrency), `src/components/studio/ChangesPanel.tsx` (I1 `expectedUpdatedAt`), active-task (closeout + post-deploy verify gate), this log.

**G3 / K1 (honest path) ÔÇö release notes for a shipped changeset ÔÇö DONE; deploy-trigger deferred (K1-deploy).** Founder ruling: K1's "gated PR" already exists (`studio.pr.open`/`studio.pr.merge`, operator-gated, J2 made merge CI-gated) and "deploy" is external (Lovable syncs `main` to Cloudflare; no Cadence deploy API), so the genuinely-new non-speculative piece is release notes. (2) `generateReleaseNotes` server fn in `studio.functions.ts`: loads the changeset's files (`studio_changes`) + commit revisions (`studio_changeset_revisions`, from I1b) + the linked work order (mission goal), then drafts GitHub-flavored markdown notes through the AI chokepoint (`callModel`, reusing the `studio` CallSurface, `google/gemini-2.5-flash`), grounded ONLY in the provided material ("no invented features"); the runtime sanitizer humanizes the output, so notes are clean by construction. Known limit: generation is owner-scoped by the existing `studio_changesets` RLS write policy (`user_id = auth.uid()`); other workspace members can read but not regenerate. **Verification:** full `bun test` 146 green, `bun run build` green. Migration applies on the next Lovable sync; the AI generation + UI need a live changeset to fully e2e. **Files:** `supabase/migrations/20260616240000_k1_release_notes.sql` new, `src/lib/studio.functions.ts` (fn + type + select + callModel import), `src/components/studio/ChangesPanel.tsx` (release-notes section), dashboard/active-task/this log.

**G3 / I1b ÔÇö Studio changeset revision history ÔÇö DONE (revert deferred). Engine lane complete.** Each `studio.commit` now records an atomic revision so the operator sees a changeset's commit history in-platform (not only on GitHub). Built: (1) migration `20260616230000_i1b_studio_revisions.sql` ÔÇö `studio_changeset_revisions` (changeset_id FK, revision_no, commit_sha, commit_url, message, files jsonb), RLS mirroring `studio_changes` (workspace via parent changeset), UNIQUE(changeset_id, revision_no) + index. (2) In `registry.server.ts` `studio.commit`, after the commit succeeds, a best-effort insert of the next revision (revision_no = count+1, sha/url/message + the file set), gated on `!outcome.cached` so an idempotency replay never double-records and wrapped in try/catch so a missing table (pre-sync) or any error never breaks shipping. (3) `getChangesetRevisions` read fn + `StudioRevision` type in `studio.functions.ts` (RLS-scoped, newest first). (4) A compact "Revisions (N)" strip in `ChangesPanel.tsx` (r-number, message, file count, short sha linking to the GitHub commit); the query degrades to a hidden strip if the table is absent pre-sync. Honest scope: **revert-to-revision is deferred** (it needs per-revision content storage or git operations; the history view is the valuable non-speculative core). **Verification:** full `bun test` 146 green, `bun run build` green. Migration applies on the next Lovable sync; UI/insert need a live commit flow to fully e2e. **G3 engine lane (I3 ÔåÆ J1 ÔåÆ J2 ÔåÆ I1 ÔåÆ I1b) is COMPLETE.** **Files:** `supabase/migrations/20260616230000_i1b_studio_revisions.sql` new, `src/lib/ai/tools/registry.server.ts` (revision insert), `src/lib/studio.functions.ts` (read fn + type), `src/components/studio/ChangesPanel.tsx` (revisions strip), dashboard/active-task/this log.

**G3 / I1 (per-hunk accept/reject) ÔÇö operator curation of a staged changeset ÔÇö DONE; revision history deferred (I1b).** Multi-file staging already shipped (`studioStage`, up to 20 files); the gap was operator control before the gated commit (all-or-nothing). Built: (1) pure `src/lib/ai/studio-hunks.ts` ÔÇö `computeHunks(base, modified)` (LCS line diff to stable-id hunks) + `applyHunkSelection(base, modified, rejectedIds)` (rejected hunks revert to base; no rejections reconstructs `modified` exactly, all rejections reconstructs `base`), 11 tests incl. round-trips, partial accept, trailing-newline, create/delete edges. (2) Two workspace-scoped server fns in `studio.functions.ts`, gated to `status='staged'` (cannot curate after commit, since the content is then on the branch): `applyStagedHunkSelection` (recompute `new_content` from the rejected set via the same pure fn the UI used, so hunk ids line up) and `rejectStagedFile` (drop a whole file). (3) `ChangesPanel.tsx` UI (engine lane owns it; the I2 watch-lane must not touch it): when the changeset is `staged`, each file shows its hunks with tap-to-reject + an Apply button, plus a Reject-file button; refetches via partial key `["studio-session"]` so it stays decoupled from the I2 route. Honest scope: "atomic revision history" (the other half of the original I1) is split out as **deferred I1b** (needs a `studio_changeset_revisions` table + commit-time snapshots, a distinct slice) rather than half-built. **Verification:** `studio-hunks.test.ts` 11/11, full `bun test` 146 green, `bun run build` green. UI interaction needs a live staged changeset to fully e2e (same limit as all Studio UI). **Engine lane (I3 ÔåÆ J1 ÔåÆ J2 ÔåÆ I1) complete.** **Files:** `src/lib/ai/studio-hunks.ts` (+`.test.ts`) new, `src/lib/studio.functions.ts` (import + 2 fns), `src/components/studio/ChangesPanel.tsx` (curation UI), dashboard/active-task/this log.

**G3 / J1 + J2 (honest path) ÔÇö test-authoring discipline + CI-green merge gate ÔÇö DONE.** Founder ruling: the Studio engine is GitHub-API-only (no Cadence execution sandbox), so a `studio.test.run` runner + `studio_test_runs` table would be speculative; tests run in the connected repo's GitHub Actions CI, which `github.ci.read` already reads. So the honest decomposition: J1 = the agent AUTHORS tests; J2 = enforce CI-green-before-merge. **J1:** migration `20260616220000_j1_studio_test_discipline.sql` rewrites the Studio (`builder`) agent system prompt to make test-authoring an explicit step (step 4 "INCLUDE TESTS", step 2 "note how the repo runs tests", step 7 "the tests you added") and restates the CI-green-before-merge loop; `CREATE OR REPLACE seed_default_agents` (other 3 agents reproduced verbatim, Studio prompt via `$studio$` dollar-quoting) for new users + a scoped `UPDATE ... WHERE slug='builder'` backfill for existing. Applies on the next Lovable sync. **J2:** new pure `src/lib/ai/studio-ci.ts` (`overallFromChecks` derives the verdict, `mergeReadinessFromCi` decides merge-readiness; 12 tests), now the single source of truth shared with `github.ci.read` (its inline derivation replaced). `studio.pr.merge` does a fresh CI read before merging and throws `MergeBlocked` while CI is red or pending (a Cadence-level gate independent of GitHub required-checks), kept outside `withIdempotency` so a blocked attempt re-checks each time and only a green merge caches. The gate is fail-safe (only ever blocks, never wrongly allows). With the J1 fix-on-red prompt, the self-correct loop closes without speculative orchestration. Known limit: a perpetually-queued check reads `pending` forever and blocks Cadence-merge (operator merges on GitHub if needed). **Verification:** `studio-ci.test.ts` 12/12, full `bun test` 135 green, `bun run build` green. Migration unverifiable live until Lovable sync (Supabase MCP unauthenticated here), like every migration in this repo. **Files:** `src/lib/ai/studio-ci.ts` (+`.test.ts`) new, `supabase/migrations/20260616220000_j1_studio_test_discipline.sql` new, `src/lib/ai/tools/registry.server.ts` (import + shared verdict + merge gate + tool description), dashboard/active-task/this log.

**G3 / I3 ÔÇö branch isolation per mission, collision-safe branch naming ÔÇö DONE.** The Studio build engine already isolates concurrent missions well: per-path `builder_file_claims` (a second mission touching the same file gets a typed `BuilderFileConflict`, claims auto-released on merge/terminal), a per-mission `studio/*` branch, idempotent commit/PR/merge, and a clean openÔåÆsquash-mergeÔåÆrelease path. The one latent isolation bug: the branch fallback `studio/${missionId.slice(0,8)}` truncated the mission UUID to 32 bits, so two concurrent missions whose UUIDs shared a leading hex prefix would compute the SAME branch and silently build on each other's head (the file-claim guard only catches same-FILE collisions, not two missions sharing a branch with different files). Fixed by binding the branch to the changeset's own UUID: new pure `src/lib/ai/studio-branch.ts` `studioBranchName(missionId, changesetId)` ÔåÆ `studio/<mission8>-<changeset12>`, an always-valid single git ref segment, now the only place the branch name is computed (`registry.server.ts` `studio.commit`). Backward-compatible: only the first-commit fallback changed; existing changesets keep their persisted `branch`, and no consumer recomputes the name (`studio.functions.ts` reads `changeset.branch` from the DB). No migration. **Verification:** new `studio-branch.test.ts` 6/6 (incl. the explicit regression: two missions sharing an 8-hex prefix now get different branches), full `bun test` 123 green, `bun run build` green. Engine-core lane, serial; next J1. **Files:** `src/lib/ai/studio-branch.ts` (+`.test.ts`) new, `src/lib/ai/tools/registry.server.ts` (import + branch line), dashboard/active-task/this log.
